         <h1 id="omnibus-gitlab-docs">Omnibus GitLab Docs<a href="#omnibus-gitlab-docs" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h1> 
         <p>Omnibus GitLab is a way to package different services and tools required to run GitLab, so that most users can install it without laborious configuration. </p>
         <h2 id="package-information">Package information<a href="#package-information" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <ul> 
          <li><a href="package-information/README.html#checking-the-versions-of-bundled-software">Checking the versions of bundled software</a> </li>
          <li><a href="package-information/defaults.html">Package defaults</a> </li>
          <li><a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/development/architecture.html#component-list">Components included</a> </li>
          <li><a href="package-information/deprecated_os.html">Deprecated Operating Systems</a> </li>
          <li><a href="package-information/signed_packages.html">Signed Packages</a> </li>
          <li><a href="package-information/deprecation_policy.html">Deprecation Policy</a> </li>
          <li><a href="https://gitlab-org.gitlab.io/omnibus-gitlab/licenses.html">Licenses of bundled dependencies</a> </li>
         </ul> 
         <h2 id="installation">Installation<a href="#installation" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <p>For installation details, see <a href="installation/index.html">Installing Omnibus GitLab</a>. </p>
         <h2 id="running-on-a-low-resource-device-like-a-raspberry-pi">Running on a low-resource device (like a Raspberry Pi)<a href="#running-on-a-low-resource-device-like-a-raspberry-pi" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2> 
         <p>You can run GitLab on supported low-resource computers like the Raspberry Pi 3, but you must tune the settings to work best with the available resources. Check out the <a href="settings/rpi.html">documentation</a> for suggestions on what to adjust. </p>
         <h2 id="maintenance">Maintenance<a href="#maintenance" title="Permalink" class="anchor"></a> </h2>

          <li><a href="maintenance/README.html#starting-a-rails-console-session">Starting a Rails console session</a> </li>
          <li><a href="maintenance/README.html#starting-a-postgresql-superuser-psql-session">Starting a PostgreSQL superuser <code class="highlighter-rouge">psql</code> session</a> </li>
          <li><a href="maintenance/README.html#container-registry-garbage-collection">Container registry garbage collection</a> </li>
         </ul>
